\"github.com/prometheus/prometheus\", \"path\": \"tsdb/wlog/wlog.go\", \"symbol\": \"Close\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"# Prometheus TSDB Write-Ahead Log (WAL) Implementation\\n\\nThe Prometheus TSDB WAL consists of a comprehensive set of Go source files in the `github.com/prometheus/prometheus` repository that implement segment-based write-ahead logging for durability and crash recovery.\\n\\n## Core WAL Segment Management (tsdb/wlog/wlog.go)\\n\\nThe main WAL implementation is in `tsdb/wlog/wlog.go`. This file contains the `WL` struct (write log) which manages WAL segments:\\n\\n- **WL struct**: The core WAL manager that handles segment creation, rotation, and record writing. Each segment is a fixed-size file (default 128MB, configurable via `WALSegmentSize` option). Segments are named sequentially as `00000000`, `00000001`, etc.\\n\\n- **Segment creation and rotation**:\\n  - `NewSize()`: Creates a new WAL with specified segment size and compression type. It initializes the first segment and creates an actor-based async worker for efficient writes.\\n  - `New()`: Convenience wrapper for NewSize using the default segment size (128MB).\\n  - `CreateSegment()`: Creates a new segment file in the WAL directory with a specified index.\\n  - `NextSegment()`: Rotates to the next segment asynchronously. This function flushes the current page, creates a new segment, and updates the write pointer.\\n  - `NextSegmentSync()`: Synchronous version of NextSegment for when immediate rotation is needed.\\n  - `SegmentName()`: Builds the filename for a segment given its index.\\n  - `Segments()`: Returns the range [first, last] of existing segments.\\n\\n- **Record writing**: The `Log()` method writes records to the WAL. Records are organized into pages (32KB) within segments. If a record doesn't fit in the current page, the page is flushed and a new page is started. If a record doesn't fit in the current segment, a new segment is automatically created.\\n\\n- **Compression**: WAL supports Snappy and Zstd compression. The compression type is specified during WAL creation and is applied selectively to individual records only if compression saves space.\\n\\n- **Segment information**: `LastSegmentAndOffset()` returns the current segment number and offset within that segment.\\n\\n## WAL Record Encoding (tsdb/record/record.go)\\n\\nThe record package defines the WAL record types and encoding/decoding:\\n\\n- **Record types** (Type enum):\\n  - `Series` (Type=1): Series labels and references\\n  - `Samples` (Type=2): Float sample values\\n  - `Tombstones` (Type=3): Deleted time ranges for series\\n  - `Exemplars` (Type=4): Exemplar data with labels\\n  - `Metadata` (Type=6): Metric metadata (unit, help text)\\n  - `HistogramSamples` (Type=7): Native histogram samples\\n  - `FloatHistogramSamples` (Type=8): Float histogram samples\\n  - `CustomBucketsHistogramSamples` (Type=9): Histograms with custom buckets\\n  - `CustomBucketsFloatHistogramSamples` (Type=10): Float histograms with custom buckets\\n  - `MmapMarkers` (Type=5): Marks for out-of-order samples that have been memory-mapped to disk\\n\\n- **Encoder struct**: Provides methods to encode series, samples, tombstones, exemplars, metadata, and histogram records:\\n  - `Series()`: Encodes series records with their labels\\n  - `Samples()`: Encodes float sample records using delta encoding for timestamps and references\\n  - `Tombstones()`: Encodes deletion markers\\n  - `Exemplars()`: Encodes exemplar data\\n  - `EncodeExemplarsIntoBuffer()`: Low-level exemplar encoding\\n  - `Metadata()`: Encodes metric metadata\\n  - `MmapMarkers()`: Encodes memory-map markers\\n  - `HistogramSamples()`: Encodes native histogram samples\\n  - `FloatHistogramSamples()`: Encodes float histogram samples\\n  - `CustomBucketsHistogramSamples()`: Encodes custom-bucket histograms\\n  - `CustomBucketsFloatHistogramSamples()`: Encodes custom-bucket float histograms\\n\\n- **Decoder struct**: Provides corresponding decode methods to read records:\\n  - `Type()`: Determines the type of a record\\n  - `Series()`: Decodes series records\\n  - `Samples()`: Decodes float samples with delta decompression\\n  - `Tombstones()`: Decodes deletion records\\n  - `Exemplars()`: Decodes exemplar data\\n  - `ExemplarsFromBuffer()`: Low-level exemplar decoding\\n  - `Metadata()`: Decodes metadata records\\n  - `MmapMarkers()`: Decodes memory-map markers\\n  - `HistogramSamples()`: Decodes histogram samples\\n  - `FloatHistogramSamples()`: Decodes float histogram samples\\n  - `DecodeLabels()`: Decodes label pairs\\n  - `DecodeHistogram()`: Decodes histogram structure\\n\\n- **Reference types**: All records reference series by a `HeadSeriesRef` (uint64) which allows efficient series tracking:\\n  - WAL Segment Management (tsdb/wlog/wlog.go)\\n\\nThe main WAL implementation is in `tsdb/wlog/wlog.go`. This file contains the `WL` struct (write log) which manages WAL segments:\\n\\n- **WL struct**: The core WAL manager that handles segment creation, rotation, and record writing. Each segment is a fixed-size file (default 128MB, configurable via `WALSegmentSize` option). Segments are named sequentially as `00000000`, `00000001`, etc.\\n\\n- **Segment creation and rotation**:\\n  - `NewSize()`: Creates a new WAL with specified segment size and compression type. It initializes the first segment and creates an actor-based async worker for efficient writes.\\n  - `New()`: Convenience wrapper for NewSize using the default segment size (128MB).\\n  - `CreateSegment()`: Creates a new segment file in the WAL directory with a specified index.\\n  - `NextSegment()`: Rotates to the next segment asynchronously. This function flushes the current page, creates a new segment, and updates the write pointer.\\n  - `NextSegmentSync()`: Synchronous version of NextSegment for when immediate rotation is needed.\\n  - `SegmentName()`: Builds the filename for a segment given its index.\\n  - `Segments()`: Returns the range [first, last] of existing segments.\\n\\n- **Record writing**: The `Log()` method writes records to the WAL. Records are organized into pages (32KB) within segments. If a record doesn't fit in the current page, the page is flushed and a new page is started. If a record doesn't fit in the current segment, a new segment is automatically created.\\n\\n- **Compression**: WAL supports Snappy and Zstd compression. The compression type is specified during WAL creation and is applied selectively to individual records only if compression saves space.\\n\\n- **Segment information**: `LastSegmentAndOffset()` returns the current segment number and offset within that segment.\\n\\n## WAL Record Encoding (tsdb/record/record.go)\\n\\nThe record package defines the WAL record types and encoding/decoding:\\n\\n- **Record types** (Type enum):\\n  -
